                        "import os\nimport csv\nimport threading\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\n\nfrom flask import Flask, render_template_string, request, jsonify, send_file\nfrom apscheduler.schedulers.background import BackgroundScheduler\nfrom werkzeug.utils import secure_filename\n\n# ---- Configuration ----\nWHATSAPP_API_URL = \"https://graph.facebook.com/v18.0/<PHONE_NUMBER_ID>/messages\"\nWHATSAPP_TOKEN = \"YOUR_WHATSAPP_BUSINESS_API_TOKEN\"\nWHATSAPP_PHONE_NUMBER_ID = \"<PHONE_NUMBER_ID>\"\nWHATSAPP_TEMPLATE_NAME = \"missed_call_reply\"  # Pre-approved template name\n\nDATA_FILE = \"call_message_log.csv\"\n\n# ---- Data Storage ----\n# In-memory log (will be loaded from CSV at startup)\nlog_data = []\n\n# ---- Flask App ----\napp = Flask(__name__)\n\n# ---- Scheduler for Message Sending ----\nscheduler = BackgroundScheduler()\nscheduler.start()\n\n# ---- Helper Functions ----\n\ndef send_whatsapp_message(phone_number, message):\n    \"\"\"\n    Send a WhatsApp message using WhatsApp Business API.\n    \"\"\"\n    import requests\n    headers = {\n        \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {WHATSAPP_TOKEN}\",\n        \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\"\n    }\n    payload = {\n        \"messaging_product\": \"whatsapp\",\n        \"to\": phone_number,\n        \"type\": \"text\",\n        \"text\": {\"body\": message}\n    }\n    response = requests.post(WHATSAPP_API_URL, json=payload, headers=headers)\n    return response.status_code, response.json()\n\ndef log_event(event_type, caller_number, message=None, scheduled_time=None):\n    \"\"\"\n    Log an event (call or message) with timestamp.\n    \"\"\"\n    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\")\n    entry = {\n        \"timestamp\": timestamp,\n        \"event_type\": event_type,\n        \"caller_number\": caller_number,\n        \"message\": message if message else \"\",\n        \"scheduled_time\": scheduled_time if scheduled_time else \"\",\n    }\n    log_data.append(entry)\n    # Append to CSV\n    write_log_to_csv(entry)\n\ndef write_log_to_csv(entry):\n    \"\"\"\n    Write a single log entry to CSV file.\n    \"\"\"\n    file_exists = os.path.isfile(DATA_FILE)\n    with open(DATA_FILE, \"a\", newline='', encoding='utf-8') as csvfile:\n        fieldnames = [\"timestamp\", \"event_type\", \"caller_number\", \"message\", \"scheduled_time\"]\n        writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=fieldnames)\n        if not file_exists:\n            writer.writeheader()\n        writer.writerow(entry)\n\ndef load_log_from_csv():\n    \"\"\"\n    Load log data from CSV file at startup.\n    \"\"\"\n    global log_data\n    if not os.path.isfile(DATA_FILE):\n        log_data = []\n        return\n    with open(DATA_FILE, \"r\", encoding='utf-8') as csvfile:\n        reader = csv.DictReader(csvfile)\n        log_data = [row for row in reader]\n\n# ---- WhatsApp Webhook Endpoint ----\n@app.route(\"/webhook\", methods=[\"POST\"])\ndef whatsapp_webhook():\n    \"\"\"\n    Endpoint to receive incoming WhatsApp webhook events.\n    Simulate missed call event by receiving a POST with caller_number.\n    \"\"\"\n    data = request.json\n    caller_number = data.get(\"caller_number\")\n    event_type = data.get(\"event_type\", \"missed_call\")\n    if not caller_number:\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"Missing caller_number\"}), 400\n\n    # Log the missed call\n    log_event(event_type, caller_number)\n\n    # Send automated reply\n    reply_message = \"Thank you for calling! We noticed you tried to reach us. How can we assist you?\"\n    status_code, resp_json = send_whatsapp_message(caller_number, reply_message)\n\n    # Log the reply message\n    log_event(\"auto_reply\", caller_number, reply_message)\n\n    return jsonify({\"status\": \"success\", \"whatsapp_api_status\": status_code, \"api_response\": resp_json})\n\n# ---- Message Scheduling ----\ndef schedule_message(phone_number, message, send_time):\n    \"\"\"\n    Schedule a WhatsApp message to be sent at a future time.\n    \"\"\"\n    def job():\n        send_whatsapp_message(phone_number, message)\n        log_event(\"scheduled_message_sent\", phone_number, message, send_time.strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\"))\n    job_id = f\"msg_{phone_number}_{send_time.timestamp()}\"\n    scheduler.add_job(job, datetime.fromisoformat(scheduled_time_str)\n    except Exception:\n        return jsonify({\"error\": \"Invalid scheduled_time format\"}), 400\n\n    schedule_message(phone_number, message,                         "import os\nimport csv\nimport threading\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\n\nfrom flask import Flask, render_template_string, request, jsonify, send_file, redirect, url_for\nfrom apscheduler.schedulers.background import BackgroundScheduler\nimport sqlite3\nimport requests\n\n# ================== CONFIGURATION ==================\nWHATSAPP_API_URL = 'https://graph.facebook.com/v17.0/<PHONE_NUMBER_ID>/messages'\nWHATSAPP_TOKEN = 'YOUR_WHATSAPP_BUSINESS_API_TOKEN'\nPHONE_NUMBER_ID = '<PHONE_NUMBER_ID>'\n\n# Automated reply message\nAUTOMATED_REPLY = \"Hi, we noticed you tried to reach us. How can we help you?\"\n\n# Flask and DB setup\napp = Flask(__name__)\nDB_FILE = 'missed_calls.db'\n\n# ================ DATABASE FUNCTIONS ================\ndef init_db():\n    \"\"\"Initialize the SQLite database and create the calls table if it doesn't exist.\"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute('''\n        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS calls (\n            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n            caller_number TEXT,\n            call_time TEXT,\n            message_sent TEXT,\n            reply_message TEXT,\n            scheduled_time TEXT\n        )\n    ''')\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef log_call(caller_number, call_time, reply_message, scheduled_time):\n    \"\"\"Log a missed call and its associated reply message and schedule.\"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute('''\n        INSERT INTO calls (caller_number, call_time, message_sent, reply_message, scheduled_time)\n        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n    ''', (caller_number, call_time, 'No', reply_message, scheduled_time))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef update_message_sent(call_id):\n    \"\"\"Mark a message as sent in the database.\"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute('UPDATE calls SET message_sent = ? WHERE id = ?', ('Yes', call_id))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef get_all_calls():\n    \"\"\"Retrieve all call logs from the database.\"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute('SELECT * FROM calls ORDER BY call_time DESC')\n    rows = c.fetchall()\n    conn.close()\n    return rows\n\ndef get_unsent_scheduled_messages():\n    \"\"\"Retrieve all scheduled messages that have not been sent yet.\"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute('''\n        SELECT id, caller_number, reply_message, scheduled_time\n        FROM calls\n        WHERE message_sent = 'No' AND scheduled_time IS NOT NULL\n    ''')\n    rows = c.fetchall()\n    conn.close()\n    return rows\n\ndef get_call_id_by_number_and_time(caller_number, call_time):\n    \"\"\"Get the call ID by caller number and call time.\"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute('SELECT id FROM calls WHERE caller_number=? send_whatsapp_message(phone_number, message):\n    \"\"\"\n    Send a WhatsApp message using the WhatsApp Business API.\n    Returns True if successful, False otherwise.\n    \"\"\"\n    headers = {\n        'Authorization': f'Bearer {WHATSAPP_TOKEN}',\n        'Content-Type': 'application/json'\n    }\n    data = {\n        \"messaging_product\": \"whatsapp\",\n        \"to\": phone_number,\n        \"type\": \"text\",\n        \"text\": {\n            \"body\": message\n        }\n    }\n    try:\n        response = requests.post(WHATSAPP_API_URL, headers=headers, json=data, timeout=10)\n        return response.status_code == 200\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error sending WhatsApp message: {e}\")\n        return False\n\n# ============== SCHEDULER FOR MESSAGES ==============\nscheduler = BackgroundScheduler()\n\ndef scheduled_message_sender():\n    \"\"\"Send scheduled WhatsApp messages whose scheduled time has arrived.\"\"\"\n    unsent = .sent { background-color: #e7e7f7;}\n    </style>\n    <script>\n        function refreshLogs() {\n            fetch('/api/logs')\n            .then(res => res.json())\n            .then(data => {\n                         "import os\nimport tempfile\nimport shutil\nimport unittest\nimport sqlite3\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\nfrom unittest.mock import patch, MagicMock\n\n# Import the app and functions from the code under test.\n# We assume the code is in a module named 'missed_call_app.py' for import.\n# For this test script, we'll simulate as if all code is present here.\n# We'll import Flask app as 'app' and the relevant DB functions.\n\n# --- Begin: Copy-paste of relevant code from the user script (with minor adjustments for testability) ---\n\nimport sys\nfrom flask import Flask, render_template_string, request, jsonify, send_file, Response\n\n# Configuration\nAUTOMATED_REPLY = \"Hi, we noticed you tried to reach us. How can we help you?\"\n\n# Flask and DB setup\napp = Flask(__name__)\nDB_FILE = 'missed_calls.db'\n\ndef init_db():\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute('''\n        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS calls (\n            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n            caller_number TEXT,\n            call_time TEXT,\n            message_sent TEXT,\n            reply_message TEXT,\n            scheduled_time TEXT\n        )\n    ''')\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef log_call(caller_number, call_time, reply_message, scheduled_time):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute('''\n        INSERT INTO calls (caller_number, call_time, message_sent, reply_message, scheduled_time)\n        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n    ''', (caller_number, call_time, 'No', reply_message, scheduled_time))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef update_message_sent(call_id):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute('UPDATE calls SET message_sent = ? WHERE id = ?', ('Yes', call_id))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef get_all_calls():\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute('SELECT * FROM calls ORDER BY call_time DESC')\n    rows = c.fetchall()\n    conn.close()\n    return rows\n\ndef get_unsent_scheduled_messages():\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute('''\n        SELECT id, caller_number, reply_message, scheduled_time\n        FROM calls\n        WHERE message_sent = 'No' AND scheduled_time IS NOT NULL\n    ''')\n    rows = c.fetchall()\n    conn.close()\n    return rows\n\ndef get_unsent_immediate_messages():\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_FILE)\n    c = conn.cursor()\n    c.execute('''\n        SELECT id, caller_number, reply_message\n        FROM For testing, this will be mocked.\n    import requests\n    headers = {\n        'Authorization': f'Bearer YOUR_WHATSAPP_BUSINESS_API_TOKEN',\n        'Content-Type': 'application/json'\n    }\n    data = {\n        \"messaging_product\": \"whatsapp\",\n        \"to\": phone_number,\n        \"type\": \"text\",\n        \"text\": {\n            \"body\": message\n        }\n    }\n    try:\n        response = requests.post(\"https://graph.facebook.com/v17.0/<PHONE_NUMBER_ID>/messages\", headers=headers, json=data, timeout=10)\n        return response.status_code == 200\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error sending WhatsApp message: {e}\")\n        return False\n\n@app.route('/api/logs')\ndef api_logs():\n    rows = get_all_calls()\n    logs = []\n    for row in rows:\n        logs.append({\n            'id': row[0],\n            'caller_number': row[1],\n            'call_time': row[2],\n            'message_sent': row[3],\n            'reply_message': row[4],\n            'scheduled_time': row[5]\n        })\n    return jsonify(logs)\n\n@app.route('/export')\ndef export_csv():\n    rows = get_all_calls()\n    def generate():\n        header = ['ID', 'Caller Number', WHERE id = ?', ('Yes', call_id))\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef get_all_calls(db_file):\n    \"\"\"Retrieve all call/message records from the database.\"\"\"\n    conn =   def api_logs():\n        rows = get_all_calls(DB_FILE)\n        logs = []\n        for row in rows:\n            logs.append({\n                'id': row[0],\n                'caller_number': row[1],\n                'call_time': row[2],\n                'message_sent': row[3],\n                'reply_message': row[4],\n                'scheduled_time': row[5]\n            })\n        return jsonify(logs)\n\n    @app.route('/export')\n    def export_csv():\n        rows = get_all_calls(DB_FILE)\n        def generate():\n            header = ['ID', 'Caller Number', 'Call Time', \"\"\"\n    headers = {\n        'Authorization': f'Bearer {WHATSAPP_TOKEN}',\n        'Content-Type': 'application/json'\n    }\n    data = {\n        \"messaging_product\": \"whatsapp\",\n
